Accessibility digest

Synopsis
PageWellTower partner StoryPoint Senior Living
URLhttps://www.storypoint.com/
Requesterpool@jpdev.pro
Test date2023/04/24
Score2017
Tested byTestaro, procedure ts24
Scored byTestilo, procedure tsp24
Digested byTestilo, procedure tdp24

Introduction

This is a digest of results from a battery of accessibility Tests.

The battery includes 1353 automated accessibility tests drawn from ten different packages: Alfa, Axe, Continuum, Equal Access, HTML CodeSniffer, Nu Html Checker, QualWeb, Tenon, Testaro, and WAVE.

These tests were run on the web page named above and gave the page a score of 2017, where 0 would be perfect.

Issue summary

Special issues

log: Score 375. This is based on the amount of browser error logging and miscellaneous logging during the tests.

preventions: Score 500. This is based on tests that the page did not allow to be run. That impedes accessibility progress and risks interfering with tools that users with disabilities need.

solos: Score 186. This is based on issues reported by unclassified tests. Details are in the report.

Classified issues

Issue focusIndication

WCAG: 2.4.7

Score: 216

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test focInd, score 214 (Focused element displays no or a nostandard focus indicator)

Issue roleBad

WCAG: 4.1.2

Score: 151

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test role, score 149 (Nonexistent or implicit-overriding role)

Issue textContrastAA

WCAG: 1.4.3

Score: 112

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package axe, test color-contrast, score 83 (Element has insufficient color contrast)
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.1_4_6.G18.Fail, score 68 (Contrast between the text and its background is less than 4.5:1)

Issue linkIndication

WCAG: 1.3.3

Score: 72

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test linkUl, score 68 (Non-underlined adjacent links)
  • Package axe, test link-in-text-block, score 4 (Link is not distinct from surrounding text without reliance on color)

Issue linkNoText

WCAG: 2.4.4

Score: 64

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package axe, test link-name, score 24 (Link has no discernible text)
  • Package continuum, test 237, score 32 (a element has no mechanism that allows an accessible name value to be calculated)
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.1_1_1.H30.2, score 12 (img element is the only link content but has no text alternative)
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.4_1_2.H91.A.NoContent, score 28 (Link has an href attribute but no text)

Issue imageNoText

WCAG: 1.1.1

Score: 51

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package axe, test image-alt, score 28 (Image has no text alternative)
  • Package continuum, test 89, score 28 (img element has no mechanism that allows an accessible name to be calculated)
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.1_1_1.H37, score 24 (img element has no alt attribute)

Issue titleBad

WCAG: 1.3.1

Score: 42

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test titledEl, score 40 (title attribute belongs to an inappropriate element)

Issue contentBeyondLandmarks

WCAG: 1.3.6

Score: 23

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package axe, test region, score 21 (Some page content is not contained by landmarks)

Issue hoverSurprise

WCAG: 1.4.13

Score: 19

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test hover, score 17 (Hovering is mis-indicated or changes content)

  • Package axe, test color-contrast-enhanced, score 4 (Element has insufficient color contrast (Level AAA))
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.1_4_6.G17.Fail, score 14 (Text has insufficient contrast)

Issue reports in this category:

Issue contrastRisk

WCAG: 1.4.3

Score: 9

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package htmlcs, test w:AAA.1_4_3_F24.F24.BGColour, score 1 (Inline background color may lack a complementary foreground color)
  • Package htmlcs, test w:AAA.1_4_3_F24.F24.FGColour, score 1 (Inline foreground color may lack a complementary background color)
  • Package htmlcs, test w:AAA.1_4_6.G17.Abs, score 4 (Contrast between the absolutely positioned text and its background may be less than 7:1)
  • Package htmlcs, test w:AAA.1_4_6.G18.Abs, score 1 (Contrast between the absolutely positioned text and its background may be less than 4.5:1)

Score: 3
